  **Headline:** *Tesla secures Texas rideshare permit for Robotaxi operation*  
  **Summary:** Tesla Robotaxi LLC has obtained a Transportation Network Company (TNC) rideshare license from the Texas Department of Licensing and Regulation. ###  Summary  
Tesla Robotaxi LLC has officially obtained a Transportation Network Company (TNC) permit from the Texas Department of Licensing and Regulation (TDLR), authorizing statewide robotaxi operations **with or without human safety drivers**, valid through August 2026. Elon Musk confirmed on X that the service will be made public in Austin as early as next month.
